 tufaani pari khilne vaale david miller ke netritv main apane ballebaajon or gendbaajon ke shandaar pradarshan ke dam par kings ilevan punjab team ne guuruuvaar ko himachal pradesh cricket sangh (echpisie) maidan par khele gaye indian premier lig (ipel) ke chathe sanskaran ke 67wein or apane 15wein mukaable main dilli dairedevills ko saat ranon se haraakar apane plaof main pahunchane kii ummiido ko kaayam rakhaa he
 For this, however, he will have to wait for the equations to come to his right
 dilli kii 15 maichon main yah 12veen haar he
 Batting first after losing the toss, Kings XI Punjab had set a target of 172 runs for victory in front of Delhi Daredevils but the Delhi team deviated from the chasing target and managed 164 runs for seven wickets in 20 overs
 punjab kii ore se sandip sharma ne teen wicket liye jabaki piyush chawla ko do safalataa mili
 Miller was voted man of the match
 is jeet ke baad kings ilevan ke 12 ank ho gaye hai
 His reach in the playoffs now depends on the defeat of Royal Challengers Bangalore and Sunrisers Hyderabad

" agar paak ye donon sharten maanata he to vah aaj raat tak jawaab de

 ' bharat ke is sawaal ke baad ab pakistan kii taraf se jawaab kaa intjaar he
 The Indian Foreign Minister categorically stated, 'pakistan's NSA Sartaj Aziz Shimla should not make the Hurriyat or anyone else a party, respecting the spirit of the agreement and do not extend the scope of the dialogue beyond terrorism, respecting the UFA consent
 agar ve iske liye raji hai, to baatcheet ke liye jarur aaen, lekin agar hurriyat se milanaa chaahate hai or kashmir par baatcheet karnaa chaahate hai to pakistan ke NSA sartaaj ajij na aaen
 However, if they agree on both these issues, then please reply by tonight, the conversation will start from tomorrow and the result will definitely come out
 videsh mantri ne sartaaj ajij ke us aarope ko bhi nakaara, jisamen unhone media ke jariye kootneeti karne kii baat kahi thi

 unhone saaf kaha, bharat-paak ke bich hone vaali har baatcheet ko vaarta nahin kaha ja saktaa
